Great hospitality. I ordered online and asked them to sit and eat there, they gladly agreed.

tl;dr Avoid this place if you want to be safe - the workers aren't wearing masks and washing hands properly, and have very bad/rude service while over charging for items.

I went there a couple of days ago for a pickup order. First, they let me and another person who was there for pickup wait for so long because the one customer service person they had preferred to answer phone calls (even the ones that came in after we arrived there) over helping the customers who are in the shop.

Second, when I gave my credit card to pay for the order that sole person helping customers charged it but didn't give me any receipt. I assumed he would have charged the right amount, but luckily I immediately got an alert from my credit card company notifying me of the charge which seemed higher than expected. There were a couple of menus on the tables up front so I quickly checked and confirmed what I was expecting was right and I was indeed over charged. When I brought this to the attention of the person there, he very rudely said "this is old menu" without showing any new menu with new prices. He came to argue with me and the other person present there without wearing his face mask properly (it was just hanging under his chin). I even requested him to wear his face mask before coming closer or talking towards us, but he completely ignored us.

While waiting for my order I saw 2 more employees - one inside the kitchen who wasn't wearing any mask or gloves of any sort, and another behind the counter packing food for pickup/delivery orders and his mask was also hanging under his chin leaving his mouth and nose exposed, and he wasn't wearing gloves either.

Given the utter lack of hygiene I saw there I just couldn't get myself to eat the food I over-paid for and I ended up throwing it just to keep myself and my family safe. PLEASE STAY AWAY IF YOU CARE ABOUT YOUR FAMILY.< /text>

All in all restaurant quality has gone down a lot.

Chaat Platter, Bhel Sundae, Chhole Bhature, Pav Bhaji, North Indian Thali, Haka Saka Noodles, Veggie Chowmein or Manchu Ping-Pong (Gobi manchurian with gravy). < review>
I moved to the Bay Area from NY and stumbled upon this restaurant while I was driving around. I was pleasantly surprised by the awesome food and lively atmosphere.  On my first visit I ordered  Chaat Platter and Papdi Poppers and instantly fell in love with the authentic taste and aroma of spicy flavors that you only find in select places in India. The service was excellent and the waiter was friendly and made me feel welcome. I have come back to Go Chaatz few more times and also brought my friends. I have tried their Gobi Manchurian, Masala Dosa and Paneer Chili Chow. Everything that we have ordered here seems to be made with care and dedication with lots of attention to detail. The restaurant has a wide selection of menu items (North & South Indian) and they even serve Paan Ice Cream which is my all time favorite!

I am giving FIVE STARS for this awesome restaurant and have been blown away by the amazing menu choice, healthy cooking and awesome service.  They are located in Fremont and I only wish they also open an additional location in San Jose.< /review>

< Review>
By far worst experience I have had at a McDonald's, If I could I would have given them half a star or no star. Traditionally I make breakfast from home but I went to this McDonald's because I wanted to try the new cinnamon roll.  When I arrived the drive-thru line was somewhat busy as it can always be because this is a popular location but I saw a sign that recommended going inside for takeout. I decided to go inside for takeout. I was the only person in line to order and there was a DoorDash person waiting as well. My order was fairly simple as I got one sausage egg McMuffin combo, an extra sausage McMuffin and both a blueberry muffin and a cinnamon roll. After about 10 minutes another DoorDash person came in and a few moments later that person's order was ready. This upset the original DoorDash person who mentioned that our orders have not been taken care of and we should have went our food first. This disgruntled door dash worker was able to get them to make his food next and then after a couple minutes they noticed I was still there so they made me what they thought was my order. When they made my order I noticed that they did not put everything in bag. I decided to open the bag in front of them to show them that the entire combo and orange juice were missing. The worker told me that I did not order a combo or orange juice so then I decided to pull up my receipt to check and was able to confirm that I ordered a combo and  an orange juice. she originally gave me the orange juice and apologize but then I mentioned what about my other breakfast sandwich and hash brown. She then told me again I did not order a combo and began to search for my order. During this whole time I noticed that my order was never put on a little screens that they use to make the orders in the back but rather they printed the receipt and just put it on the counter. Eventually after finding my receipt she then grabbed a hash brown and another sandwich.

All in all this location is not organized. They prioritize the drive-thru and DoorDash orders. The drive-thru is always busy so they want you to come in to make a delivery/takeout order but you have to watch them to make sure that you get what you pay for and that they make it correctly.

On a separate note I I must have been there over 20 minutes for this order and witnessed some type of  shift change over which is partially why try to express patience with them but the team members that were leaving seem more concerned about making their own orders to go home than helping any customers and both team members that came into did not wear a mask upon entering but rather waited until someone said something to then put on their mask. In my opinion this is very rude of a staff that expects this of their customers.< /Review>
